SRIC TYPIC/AMBUD/Operational

AMTRIGON-8 (201-283995), AMBUD Case #97

ALTAN RIQUIRLO". AUCRINCES

Reference:

UFGW-7010, 29 Apr11 1968

AMTRIGON-8 was a member of the VILLARO creW.

During

May 1962 he clandestinely and without authorization boarded an

infiltration craft moments before its departure on an

operational mission.

absence was not discovered until the

team had infiltrated and moved into its first position.

In 8 or 9 June 1962 the infiltration team, including

AMTRIGON-8,

became envared in a firefight with a militia

or perhaps captured.

However, no further word has been heard

from AMTRIGON-8 and he is presumed to be dead.

Taking into consideration that the disposition of thig

could have an allect on the morale of the other crew

members and their attitude toward worlk.,

it was decided to

advise the.widow of AMTRIGON-8 that he died a hero's death--

while fighting for the liberation of his country and to continue

monthly payments to the widow and children for an indefinite

Inclusion of Subject's name

on AMBUD Hero & Martyr

was deemed to be the most suitable and expeditious manner

in which to handle such payments.

The response to paragraph 2 of reference will be

the subject of a separate dispatch.

Distribution:

AMTIKI-I has contacted the bank regarding the Social

Security numbers requested and has been advised that, although

the bank is not obligated to insist upon Social Security or other

identifying numbers for these accounts, it does feel that AMTIKI-1

may ultimately be subjected to an inquiry.

the Internal Revenue

Their reasoning is based primarily upon

the fact that

while trust accounts for our purposes, are not true

trust accounts in that no trust agreements

are of record at

(Trust agreements could

of course, since the

Individuals were not and are not available to sign.)

2.

In order to protect ANTIKI-l from any possible IRS

investigation and, rather than pursue

bank, for which we have, no cleared contact, it is suggested that

these accounts be closed out over a two or

re-éstablished at Headquarters through the appropriate DTEARN

channels.

If the accounts remain here, it will be necessary to

preyare new signature cards for each account removing Humphrey O.

TINANUS as a signatory and adding a JMCOBRA asset as an "inside"

trustee for control purposes, or to remove ANTIKI-l entirely and

establish the JNCOBRA asset as the sole trustee.

3. Please advise.

STALLANS

Sir:

Attention: Mr. Administrator

I am

writing to you to ask you to do me the favor of informing

Nr. John Paulbath

thot I urgently need him to contact me because

I want him to send the passages to me to go (to the U.S. ) via Spain.

The reason I have taken the liberty of writing is that in

Novamber of last year, I wrote to Mr.

Paulbath at PO Box 127, Tamiamt

Station in that city and after almost six months the letter was

returned to me with the notation that the address was not registered.

Since that timo a triend of mine who lives in Los Angeley has veen

trying to locate him and to date has had no success.

Mr: Paulbath sent me a notice informing that the monthly stipend

due me (as a result

death of my husband)

per dotal policy 1023,.

was being deposited in

that bank, enclosed is that notice.

last news. I liad from Mr. Paulbath was in February 1966 when he informed

me that on that date the account showed a balance of US $12, 518.21.

I appeal to your kindness for help,

since I have been trying

for moro than

six

years

since my husband died

R.I.P. to leave (Cuba).

I atsmos almost had all my papers in order to leave when the American

Embassy was closed that was

two months after my husband had departed

(Cuba),

later

in Apri1. of

that same year came the Bay of Pigs Invasion

and my husband was killed.

On 1 June my daughter was,

born and it

though"?

a passport for my daughter since to obtain it they demanded my husband's

death certificate and his death was not recorded in any court, I went

to all the places it could have been recorded.

Then I began to visit

lawyers and government offices to find out how I could obtain a passport

for my

daughter.

After much fighting,

It was delivered to me at the

end of November of last year. I immediately grote to sir. Paulbath

to ask that he

send me the money for passages right aray and that was

the letter that was returned to me.

Since letters from there to here take so long, I request that

you tell Mr. Paulbath to send me the money for passages for those

indicated below:

TRANSIATION

Chicago, May 6, 1967

Dear Mr. _

In your letter of I May 1967 you asked me for my

marriage.

certificato and my son's birth certificate, I do not have them

because my home was immediately intervened by the so-called

Comandanto Felix Torres who burned my family passport and wouldn't

-----

even let me get my son's clothing. My cousin (?), Porf1r10's

brother Rodolfo RAMIREZ sine clandestinely went to the coasts of

Cuba to get me. I am sending you photostatic copios of our .

parolee cards. I bellove they will suffico but at tho samo time

I will arite to Porfirio's mother who is still in Cuba since

she has not been given permission to leave and come to this country

and I will ask her to get coples of the marriage certificato.

I will send them to you as soon as I receive them.

Thanks again,

As/ Clara DELGADO

CUBAN DEMOCRATIC REVCLUTIONARY FRONT

FINANCE DEPARTMENT

RESUME OF THE INCOME AND EXPENSES OPERATIONS

"PAULA AND SOSA"

October 1 to 31, 1960

In the financial statements and annex the analysis and sub-analysis of

each one of the income and liabilities during the month of October are

shown.

Receipts, invoices, deposit

slips and other papers are kept in our files.

As shown on Annex "I-D", a Revolving Fund has been created for the M1l1-

tary Section, anounting to the sume of 310, 000.00, divided into two parts

of $5,000.00

each, the amount of $3,387.81, was reinbursed to this Revoly

1ng Fund, as per Annex "I-D".

The amount of $50,000.00 which appears as "Transferenceg" in Annex *I-M»

corresponds to the transfered amount from the account of "Paula and Sosa"

to "Rasco and Paula" account.

From this amount, we have paid in advance the November payment of the

military dependants.

In relation to "Checks to Justify", amounting to $69,288.52, as per -

Annex "I-P", these could be classified in two groups; one formed by -

those corresponding to amounts advanced accoiding to budget to the

different Committees and Delegations and the other, formed by certain

expenses to be made, but specifically determined, with receipts dully

signed. The later could have been distributed to those accounts with-

in the cassification, thus eliminating them from the title "to justify",

but have been kept as so, to be sure of the making of this expense for

the purpose to which the checks were drown for, or its actual classific-

ation, if these expense were made for other purposes than those original-

ly aimed to.

This is due to the fact that some checks were drawn for a

specific purpose; they could also have been applied to acquire some

other asset, thus appearing at the end of the month a alse balance, since

It would appear as an expense, what it actually is an asset.

Section designated as "Transferences" $50,000.00 19 compensuleu with an

Income for the same arount, when making a transference of lunds to the

"Pasco and Paula" account. to pay through it the payroll of the Military

Dependarts, but through a mistake it was jeposited again in the same

account.

GRIBBAL

Henos tratado, cumpliendo las innirecciores reelbides, de rendir en lalor

se de las operaciones del vos da lgosto, que se ajaste lo no posible a las so

cosidados regueridas, y que abarque la suyor cantidad posible de intornacion a

tachon de los recibos, facturas, etco, joe ya se esta experando, pues se bos
